ta.localStorage.set('qualaroo-page-views', views);
} else {
ta.localStorage.set('qualaroo-session-id', currentSessionId);
ta.localStorage.set('qualaroo-page-views', 1);
}
}
</script>

ta.queueForLoad(function () {
detectChromeExtension(null, function () {
detectPinterestBrowserButton(checkPinterestGrid, null);
})
});
function detectChromeExtension( installedCallback, notInstalledCallback ) {
var img = new Image();
img.src = "chrome-extension://oiekdmlabennjdpgimlcpmphdjphlcha/images/owl-48.png";
img.onload = function() { installedCallback && installedCallback(); };
img.onerror = function() { notInstalledCallback && notInstalledCallback(); };
}
function detectPinterestBrowserButton(installedCallback, notInstalledCallback) {
var img = new Image();
img.src = "chrome-extension://gpdjojdkbbmdfjfahjcgigfpmkopogic/img/icon_48.png";
img.onload = function() { installedCallback && installedCallback(); };
img.onerror = function() { notInstalledCallback && notInstalledCallback() };
}
function checkPinterestGrid() {
var searchTarget = document.body;
var ceOverlay = document.querySelector('#CEPP');
var observer = new MutationObserver(function (mutations) {
mutations.forEach(function (mutation) {
mutation.addedNodes.forEach(function (node) {
if (node.tagName === 'IFRAME' && /gpdjojdkbbmdfjfahjcgigfpmkopogic\/html\/(grid|search|create)\.html/.test(node.src)) {
node.style.zIndex = 10500;
ceOverlay.style.display = 'block';
if (node.src.indexOf('/html/grid.html') > 0) {
ceOverlay.classList.remove('search', 'create');
ta.trackEventOnPage('ce_pinterest_promo', 'pinterest_activated', 'grid');
}
else if (node.src.indexOf('/html/search.html') > 0) {
ceOverlay.classList.remove('create');
ceOverlay.classList.add('search');
ta.trackEventOnPage('ce_pinterest_promo', 'pinterest_activated', 'search');
}
else if (node.src.indexOf('/html/create.html') > 0) {
ceOverlay.classList.remove('search');
ceOverlay.classList.add('create');
ta.trackEventOnPage('ce_pinterest_promo', 'pinterest_activated', 'create');
}
}
});
mutation.removedNodes.forEach(function (node) {
if (node.tagName == 'IFRAME' && node.src.indexOf('gpdjojdkbbmdfjfahjcgigfpmkopogic') > 0) {
ceOverlay.style.display = 'none';
}
});
});
});
observer.observe(searchTarget, { childList: true });
ta.trackEventOnPage('ce_pinterest_promo', 'pinterest_detected');
}
</script>

, _checkoutElement = api.find('[data-datetype=CHECKOUT]', widget.element)
;
function _setDateLabel(target, date) {
var label;
var dateFormat = target.getAttribute("data-dateFormat");
if (!date) {
label = target.getAttribute('data-emptyText');
api.addClass(target, 'no-date'); /* HOT-4572 */
} else {
label = ta.i18n.formatDate(dateFormat, date);
api.removeClass(target, 'no-date');  /* HOT-4572 */
}
api.find('.picker-inner .picker-label', target).firstChild.nodeValue = label; /* HOT-4599 */
}
function _onDateSelected(target, dateType, date) {

} else if (dateType === 'CHECKOUT') {
_setDateLabel(_checkoutElement, date[0]);
} else if (dateType === 'STAYDATES') {
_setDateLabel(_checkinElement, date[0]);
_setDateLabel(_checkoutElement, date[1]);
}
}

}, 'datepicker widget handlers');

require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {
var define = placements.define.bind(placements,'background_update_dates','handlers',['handlers']);
/**
* Poll travel info cookie for updated dates, and if found, update page
*/
define(['placement', 'lib/jquery-amd', 'utils/cookieutils', 'ta/page'],
function(placement, $, CookieUtils, page) {
var _timeToPoll = 2 * 1000; // poll every 2 seconds
var _timeToTimeout = 15 * 60 * 1000; // timeout after 15 minutes
var _checkin = getTravelDate('A');
var _checkout = getTravelDate('D');
var _polling;
var _timeout;
/**
* Get a travel date from the cookie.
* @param {String} prefix
* @returns {Date}
*/
function getTravelDate(prefix) {
var day, month, year;
day = getTravelInfoItem(prefix + 'D');
month = getTravelInfoItem(prefix + 'M');
year = getTravelInfoItem(prefix + 'Y');
if (day && month && year) {
return dateFromString(year + '/' + month + '/' + day);
}
return null;
}
/**
* Get a travel info item from the cookie.
* @param {String} key
* @returns {String}
*/
function getTravelInfoItem(key) {
var travelInfoCookie = CookieUtils.getCookie('TATravelInfo');
if (travelInfoCookie) {
var travelInfo = travelInfoCookie.split('*');
for (var i = 0; i < travelInfo.length; i++) {
var item = travelInfo[i].split('.');
if (item[0] === key) {
return item[1];
}
}
}
}
/**
* Convert a date string formatted as year/month/day into a Date object.
* @param {String} dateString
* @returns {Date}
*/
function dateFromString(dateString) {
var components = dateString.split('/');
return new Date(parseInt(components[0]), parseInt(components[1]) - 1, parseInt(components[2]));
}
/**
* Compares passed in dates with current dates and returns passed in dates if they are different from current dates.
* @param {[Date, Date]} dates
* @returns ({[Date, Date]})
*/
function checkForUpdatedDates(dates) {
if (!dates || dates.length != 2) {
return;
}
var checkin = dates[0];
var checkout = dates[1];
if (checkin instanceof Date && checkout instanceof Date) {
// make sure we're ignoring time
checkin.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
checkout.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
if (_checkin instanceof Date && _checkout instanceof Date) {
// make sure we're ignoring time
_checkin.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
_checkout.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
// compare the dates and return the updated dates if they have changed
if (checkin.getTime() != _checkin.getTime() || checkout.getTime() != _checkout.getTime()) {
return [checkin, checkout];
}
}
else {
// no old dates, so just return the new dates
return [checkin, checkout];
}
}
}
/**
* Updates the page (sets datepickers and fetches updated prices) with the passed in dates.
* @param {[Date, Date]} dates
*/
function pushDates(dates) {
page.pushDates(document.querySelector('body'), 'STAYDATES', [dates[0], dates[1]]);
}
/**
* Event handler for 'dateSelected' page event.
* @param {Element} target
* @param {String} dateType
* @param {[Date, Date]} dates
*/
function dateSelected(target, dateType, dates) {
if (dateType == 'STAYDATES') {
if (checkForUpdatedDates(dates)) {
stopPolling(); // user changed dates in this tab
}
}
}
/**
* Check travel info cookie for updated dates (changed in a different tab).
*/
function poll() {
if (_polling) {
var dates = checkForUpdatedDates([getTravelDate('A'), getTravelDate('D')]);
if (dates) {
pushDates(dates);
stopPolling(); // dates were updated in a different tab
}
else {
setTimeout(poll, _timeToPoll);
}
}
}
/**
* Starts polling of the travel info cookie for updated dates.
*/
function startPolling() {
_polling = true;
poll();
if (!_timeout) {
_timeout = setTimeout(function () {
stopPolling(); // timeout out
}, _timeToTimeout);
}
}
/**
* Pauses polling of the travel info cookie.
* Clears the interval and timeout.
*/
function pausePolling() {
_polling = false;
clearTimeout(_timeout);
_timeout = null;
}
/**
* Stops polling of the travel info cookie.
* Clears the interval and timeout.
* Removes the event handlers.
*/
function stopPolling() {
pausePolling();
page.off('dateSelected', dateSelected);
$(window).off('blur', startPolling);
$(window).off('focus', pausePolling);
}
// Setup the event handlers to start polling on blur, pause on focus, and stop when dates have been updated.
// Assumes we have default dates, otherwise placement would have been featured off by FeatureDefaultDates.java.
page.on('dateSelected', dateSelected);
$(window).on('blur', startPolling);
$(window).on('focus', pausePolling);
}
);
});require(['ta/p13n/placements','ta/page','$prp/background_update_dates/handlers'], function(placements, impl) {
window.ta.plc_background_update_dates_handlers = placements.load('background_update_dates','handlers.js', { 'name': 'background_update_dates', 'id': 'taplc_background_update_dates', 'location_id': 237059, 'servletClass': 'com.TripResearch.servlet.accommodation.AccommodationDetail', 'servletName': 'Hotel_Review', 'params': {}, 'data': {}});});
require(['ta/prwidgets'], function(widgets) {

define(['widget', 'vanillajs', 'ta/common/Flyout', 'ta/Core/TA.Record', 'ta/util/Link', 'ta/Core/TA.Event', 'overlays/uiOverlay', 'ta/maps/opener'],
function (widget, vanillajs, taFlyout, taRecord, taLink, taEvent, uiOverlay, mapsOpener) {
var dataElem = document.querySelector('.blRow');
function _onWebLinkClicked(event, target) {
if (!dataElem) {
return;
}
var locId = dataElem.getAttribute('data-locid');
var targetHref = target.getAttribute('data-ahref');
var trackingKey = target.getAttribute('data-trackingkey') || 'URL_HOTEL';

'newTab': true
};

}
function _onEmailClicked(event, target) {

}
function _onMenuClicked(event, target) {
_fireScrollEvents('TABS_MENU');

}
function _onAddressHovered(event, target) {

}
}
function _onAddressClicked(event, target) {

mapFilters && (mapOptions.customFilters = mapFilters.split(','));

}
function _fireTracking(target, contactType) {

var locId = dataElem.getAttribute('data-locid');
var column = target.getAttribute('data-column');
var gaAction = contactType+"|text|" + column + "||";
taRecord.trackEventOnPage(gaContext, gaAction, locId, 0, false);

});require(['ta/prwidgets'], function(widgets) {
var define = widgets.define.bind(widgets,'meta_hsx_price_drawer_structured','handlers',['deferred/animate','trcss!deferred/content','handlers']);
define(["widget", "lib/jquery-amd", "ta/Core/TA.Store", "ta/Core/TA.Event"],
function(widget, $, store, taEvent) {
var $allOffers
, $items
, $priceDrawerContainer
, _priceDrawerId  // A unique id for storing price drawer state
, _locationId
, _numsKey = 'hotels_expanded_inline_nums'
, _valid = false
;
function viewAll(onlyOpen) {
widget.require(["trjs!deferred/animate", "trcss!deferred/content"], function(animate, content) {
if (_valid) {
if (animate.isExpanded()) {
if (onlyOpen) {
return;
}
collapse();
}
else {
animate.expand(true);
recordEvent('price_drawer_open', 'Price_Drawer', _priceDrawerId, $items.length);
}
}
});
}
function showMore() {
widget.require(["trjs!deferred/animate", "trcss!deferred/content"], function(animate, content) {
if (_valid) {
animate.incrementNumOffersToShow();
animate.updateMore(true);
recordEvent('price_drawer_show_more', 'Price_Drawer', _priceDrawerId, getNumOffersToShow());
}
});
}
function collapse() {
widget.require(["trjs!deferred/animate", "trcss!deferred/content"], function(animate, content) {
if ($priceDrawerContainer && animate.isExpanded()) {
$priceDrawerContainer.removeClass('expanded');
animate.resetNumOffersToShow();
animate.collapseAnimation();
recordEvent('price_drawer_collapse', 'Price_Drawer', _priceDrawerId, getNumOffersToShow());
}
});
}
function recordEvent(event, component, id, numOffers) {
widget.require(['trjs!ta/Core/TA.Record'], function(taRecord) {
taRecord.trackEventOnPage(event, component, id, numOffers);
});
}
function getNumOffersToShow() {
var nums = getAllNumOffersToShow();
var num = nums[_priceDrawerId];
num = num || 0;
if (!$items) {
return 0;
}
return num;
}
function getAllNumOffersToShow() {
var nums = store.retrieve(_numsKey);
if (!nums) {
nums = {};
}
return nums;
}
function resetToStandardHeight() {
widget.require(["trjs!deferred/animate", "trcss!deferred/content"], function(animate, content) {
animate.resetNumOffersToShow();
animate.expand(true);
});
}
// Initialize the widget with the correct state
$allOffers = $(widget.element).find(".allOffers");
if ($allOffers.length) {
$priceDrawerContainer = $allOffers.closest('[data-pricedrawer]');
$items = $('li', $allOffers);
_locationId = $allOffers.data("locationid");
if ($priceDrawerContainer.length) {
_priceDrawerId = _locationId + "_" + $priceDrawerContainer.attr('data-pricedrawer');
_valid = true;
}
}
if (_valid && $allOffers.length) {
if (getNumOffersToShow()) {
widget.require(["trjs!deferred/animate", "trcss!deferred/content"], function(animate, content) {
animate.expand(false);
});
}
}
// Set event listeners
$priceDrawerContainer.off("viewAllPriceDrawerToggle");
$priceDrawerContainer.on("viewAllPriceDrawerToggle", function(){viewAll(false)});
$priceDrawerContainer.off("viewAllPriceDrawerOpen");
$priceDrawerContainer.on("viewAllPriceDrawerOpen", function(){viewAll(true)});
taEvent.off("closeAllPriceDrawers");
taEvent.on("closeAllPriceDrawers", collapse);
taEvent.off("setPriceDrawerStandardHeight");
taEvent.on("setPriceDrawerStandardHeight", resetToStandardHeight);
return {
viewAll: viewAll,
showMore: showMore,
collapse: collapse
};

Track.record(actionPrefix + action);
}

define('common/Radio', ['vanillajs'], function(){
var RADIOS = {};
var SPLITTER = /\s+/;
function Radio(channel){
this.channel = channel;
this.events = {};
this.replies = {};
}
Radio.prototype.reply = function(name, callback, context){
name.split(SPLITTER).forEach(function(n){
this.replies[n] || (this.replies[n] = []);
this.replies[n].push({
callback: callback,
context: context || this
});
}, this);
return this;
};
Radio.prototype.request = function(name){
if (!this.replies[name]){ return null; }
var args = [].slice.call(arguments, 1);
var r = this.replies[name];
r = r[r.length - 1];
return r.callback.apply(r.context, args);
};
Radio.prototype.requestMany = function(name){
if (!this.replies[name]){ return null; }
var args = [].slice.call(arguments, 1);
return this.replies[name].map(function(r){
return r.callback.apply(r.context, args);
});
};
Radio.prototype.requestAll = function(name, expected){
if (!this.replies[name]){ return true; }
var args = [].slice.call(arguments, 1);
var fn = typeof expected == 'function' ? expected : function(v){ return v === expected; };
return this.replies[name].reduce(function(b, r){
return b && fn(r.callback.apply(r.context, args));
}, true);
};
Radio.prototype.requestEvery = Radio.prototype.requestAll;
Radio.prototype.requestAny = function(name, expected){
if (!this.replies[name]){ return false; }
var args = [].slice.call(arguments, 1);
var fn = typeof expected == 'function' ? expected : function(v){ return v === expected; };
return this.replies[name].reduce(function(b, r){
return b || fn(r.callback.apply(r.context, args));
}, false);
};
Radio.prototype.requestSome = Radio.prototype.requestAny;
Radio.prototype.on = function(name, callback, context){
name.split(SPLITTER).forEach(function(n){
this.events[n] || (this.events[n] = []);
this.events[n].push({
callback: callback,
context: context || this
});
}, this);
return this;
};
Radio.prototype.once = function(name, callback, context){
name.split(SPLITTER).forEach(function(n){
this.events[n] || (this.events[n] = []);
this.events[n].push({
callback: callback,
context: context || this,
single: true
});
}, this);
return this;
};
Radio.prototype.one = Radio.prototype.once;
Radio.prototype.off = function(name, callback){
name.split(SPLITTER).forEach(function(n){
if (!this.events[n]) {return;}
this.events[n] = this.events[n].filter(function(o){
return callback && o.callback != callback;
});
}, this);
return this;
};
Radio.prototype.trigger = function(name){
if (!this.events[name]) {return;}
var args = [].slice.call(arguments, 1);
this.events[name] = this.events[name].filter(function(o){
o.callback.apply(o.callback, args);
return !o.single;
});
return this;
};
Radio.prototype.emit = Radio.prototype.trigger;
return function(channel){
return (RADIOS[channel] || (RADIOS[channel] = new Radio(channel)));
};
});
require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {
var define = placements.define.bind(placements,'global_nav','handlers',['deferred/lateHandlers','handlers']);
/* jshint newcap:false */
define([
'placement',
'lib/jquery-amd',
'common/Radio'
], function(
placement,
$,
Radio
) {
'use strict';
var placementEl = $('#' + placement.id);
var radio = Radio('global-nav');
var oldOverlay = null;
var mastheadSavesApp = null;
// Trigger in 'placements/global_nav_action_trips/handlers'
radio.on('run-my-trips-test-3', function() {
openMyTrips(false, true);
});
// Update Global Nav content
var _onSuccessLoginRefresh = (function(response) {
window.userLoggedIn = true;
// Update the masthead, but keep some of the old content.
// This is because the AJAX servlet does not generate the correct content
// for the original page (instead, it generates it for /MetaPlacementAjax).
// Note this uses the IDs to match each "old" element with its corresponding "new" element.
var oldMenus = $("<div>").append(placementEl.find('.global-nav-no-refresh'));
placementEl.html(response);
placementEl.find('.global-nav-no-refresh').each(function(idx, el) {
$(el).replaceWith(oldMenus.find('#' + el.getAttribute('id'))[0]);
});
if (oldOverlay) {
oldOverlay.hide('replace-el');
}
}).bind(placementEl);
var _getRequestOptionsForLoginRefresh = function() {
return {
// This should not be necessary, but for some reason placements
// seems tightly coupled with the location store
skipLocation: placement.location_id <= 0,
returnTo: document.location.pathname + (document.location.search||'') + (document.location.hash||'')
};
};
// When login state changes, request the updated global nav
$(document).on('regOverlay:success', function() {
placement.requestAJAXPlacement( _onSuccessLoginRefresh, null, _getRequestOptionsForLoginRefresh());
});
// When mousing over the global nav links, show their submenus
placementEl.on('mouseenter', '.global-nav-links-container [data-element]', function(evt) {
var elmt = $(this);
var linkEl = elmt.find('a').first();
if (oldOverlay) {
oldOverlay.hide('new-overlay');
}
// Is there a submenu to show?
var menuEl = placementEl.find(elmt.data('element')).clone();
if (!menuEl.length) {
return;
}
var reqs = ['trjs!overlays/Overlay',
'trjs!overlays/styles/flyout',
'trjs!overlays/options/closeOnMouseAway',
'trjs!overlays/position',
'trjs!overlays/options/destroyOnHide'
];
require(reqs, function(Overlay, Flyout, CloseOnMouseAway, Position, DestroyOnHide) {
var overlay = new Overlay(elmt[0], new Flyout(menuEl[0], 'global-nav-flyout global-nav-menu'), CloseOnMouseAway, Position.bottomRight([0, 1]), DestroyOnHide);
overlay.domParent = placementEl.find('.global-nav-overlays-container')[0];
overlay.show();
// For tracking clicks to submenu links, we add an attribute to the link being hovered over so we can retrieve
// the tracking prefix from the link's tracking-label attribute.
linkEl.attr('data-active-menu-trigger', true);
$(evt.currentTarget).find('.ui_tab').addClass('hovering');
overlay.on('hide', function() {
// Remove attribute used for tracking
linkEl.removeAttr('data-active-menu-trigger');
$(evt.currentTarget).find('.ui_tab').removeClass('hovering');
});
oldOverlay = overlay;
});
});
// When mousing over a menu in the dropdown, open the submenu
placementEl.on('mouseenter', '.expandSubItem', function(evt) {
var elmt = $(this);
// CX-2715 avoid opening a duplicate submenu
if (elmt.hasClass('active')) {
return;
}
elmt.addClass('active');
elmt.siblings('.expandSubItem').removeClass('active');
var submenuEl = elmt.find('.secondSubNav').clone();

'trjs!overlays/styles/flyout',
'trjs!overlays/options/closeOnMouseOut',
'trjs!overlays/options/destroyOnHide'
];
require(reqs, function(Overlay, Flyout, CloseOnMouseOut, DestroyOnHide) {
var overlay = new Overlay(elmt[0], new Flyout(submenuEl[0]), CloseOnMouseOut, DestroyOnHide);
overlay.domParent = targetEl[0];
submenuEl.css('display', 'block');
overlay.show();
});
});
// If we're opening the more menu, add any elements that are hidden or collapsed due to space
placementEl.on('mouseenter', '.global-nav-links-ellipsis', function(evt) {

menuEl.prepend(elsToShow);
var reqs = ['trjs!overlays/Overlay',
'trjs!overlays/styles/flyout',
'trjs!overlays/options/closeOnMouseAway',
'trjs!overlays/position',
'trjs!overlays/options/destroyOnHide'
];
require(reqs, function(Overlay, Flyout, CloseOnMouseAway, Position, DestroyOnHide) {

});

overlay.domParent = placementEl.find('.global-nav-overlays-container')[0];
overlay.show();
elm.addClass('menu-open');
$(evt.currentTarget).find('.ui_icon').addClass('hovering');
overlay.on('hide', function() {
elm.removeClass('menu-open');
$(evt.currentTarget).find('.ui_icon').removeClass('hovering');
});
oldOverlay = overlay;
});
});
// Trackng: Logo clicks
placementEl.on('click', '.global-nav-logo', function() {
require(['trjs!ta/Core/TA.Record'], function(taRecord) {
taRecord.setEvtCookie('TopNav', 'click', 'TAlogo', 0, '/Home');

// Mobile Web Global Nav Persistent Icons
function checkForPersistentIcons() {
var showLogo = $('.first-view', placementEl);
var hideLogo = $('.second-view', placementEl);
var offsetPosition = $(window).scrollTop();
var persistentIcons = $('.persistent-icons', placementEl);
var navIcons = $('.global-nav-icons', persistentIcons);
if (navIcons.length) {
var logo = $('.global-nav-logo');
var pill = $('[data-placement-name="global_nav_geopill"]');
// A - Sideways default state: Logo and icons together, geo pill on second line
// B - Sideways 1st scroll (down): Icons animate to geo pill, logo scrolls out of view
// C - Sideways 2nd scroll (down): Icons locked to geo pill, all elements scroll out of view
//
// A - Internal default state: No logo, geo pill and icons on first line
// B - Internal 1st scroll (down): Icons locked to geo pill, all elements scroll out of view
//
// Adjust icons to placements: Logo then Geopill when available
if (pill.is(':visible')) {
if (offsetPosition < 0) {
navIcons.css({
'top': 0
});
}
else if (offsetPosition >= 0 && offsetPosition <= persistentIcons.height() - pill.height()) {
navIcons.css({
'top': offsetPosition
});
}
}
}
}
// Auto scroll to desired position based on traffic type
function positionSecondView() {
var showLogo = $('.first-view', placementEl);
var hideLogo = $('.second-view', placementEl);
var offsetPosition = $(window).scrollTop();
var persistentIcons = $('.persistent-icons', placementEl);
var navIcons = $('.global-nav-icons', persistentIcons);
if (navIcons.length) {
var logo = $('.global-nav-logo');
var pill = $('[data-placement-name="global_nav_geopill"]');
if (hideLogo.length && pill.is(':visible')) {
offsetPosition = persistentIcons.height() - logo.height();
window.scroll(0, offsetPosition);
navIcons.css({
'position': 'absolute',
'top': 'auto',
'bottom': 0
});
}
}
}
// Global Nav Persistent Single-line Header
function checkForPersistentGlobalNav() {
var persistentGlobalNav = $('.global-nav-persistent', placementEl);
if (persistentGlobalNav.length) {
persistentGlobalNav.toggleClass('fixed', $(window).scrollTop() > placementEl.offset().top);
}
}
require(['trjs!ta/Core/TA.Event'], function(taEvent) {
taEvent.queueForLoad( function() {
positionSecondView();
});
});
window.onscroll = function() {
require(['trjs!utils/throttle'], function(throttle) {
throttle(checkForPersistentIcons(), 0);
throttle(checkForPersistentGlobalNav(), 100);
});
};
return {
checkForPersistentIcons: checkForPersistentIcons,
checkForPersistentGlobalNav: checkForPersistentGlobalNav
};
});

define('Logging', ['vanillajs'], function(vanilla) {
var DEBUG_LEVEL = typeof IS_DEBUG !== 'undefined' && IS_DEBUG ? 3 : -1;
var result = {};
var levels = ['error', 'warn', 'dir', 'info', 'debug'];
for (var i=0; i<levels.length; i++) {
var level = levels[i];
result[level] = (function(level, idx) {
return function() {
if (DEBUG_LEVEL < idx) {
return;
}
if (typeof console === 'undefined' || !console[level] || !console[level].apply) {
return;
}
console[level].apply(console, arguments);
}
})(level, i);
}
result.setLevel = function(newLevel) {
DEBUG_LEVEL = newLevel;
};
return result;
});
define('common/DustRenderer', ['Logging'], function(Logging) {
return function(template, data) {
var dustGlobal = {};
if (require.defined('page-model')) {
dustGlobal = require('page-model').DUST_GLOBAL;
} else {
dustGlobal = DUST_GLOBAL;
}
if (!template || !dust.cache[dustGlobal.LOCALE + template]) {
throw new Error('Template is missing for ' + template);
}
var start = new Date().getTime();
var blob = dust.makeBase(dustGlobal).push(data);
var output = '';
dust.render(dustGlobal.LOCALE + template, blob, function (err, out) {
if (err) {
throw err;
}
output = out;
});
var totalTime = (new Date().getTime() - start);
if (totalTime > 5) {
Logging.warn('Template ' + template + ' took ' + totalTime + 'ms to render');
}
return output;
};
});
define('overlays/styles/flyout', ['vanillajs', 'api-mod'], function(vanilla, api) {
'use strict';
function buildDOM(classes) {
this.container = api.createElement('div', {
'class': 'ui_overlay ui_flyout' + (classes ? ' ' + classes : '')
});
this.contentElement = this.container;
}
var Overlay = function(content, classes) {
return function() {
buildDOM.call(this, classes || this.sourceElement.getAttribute('data-flyout') || '');
this.updateContent(content);
};
};
return Overlay;
});
define('overlays/options/destroyOnHide', ['vanillajs'], function(vanilla){
return function() {
this.hide = function(hideTrigger) {
if (!this.container.overlay) {
return;
}
delete this.container.overlay;
this.domParent.removeChild( this.container );
this.emit('hide', { trigger: hideTrigger });
this.emit('destroy', { trigger: hideTrigger });
this.sourceElement = null;
this.contentElement = null;
return this;
};
};
});
define('overlays/options/fade', ['lib/jquery-amd'], function($){
'use strict';
var NOOP = function(){};
var fadeInClass = 'fade_in';
var fadeOutClass = 'fade_out';
function addClass(cl){
$(this.container).addClass(cl);
$(this.shade).addClass(cl);
}
function removeClass(cl){
$(this.container).removeClass(cl);
$(this.shade).removeClass(cl);
}
var BOTH = [
function(fadeType){
addClass.call(this, fadeType.cl);
},
function(fadeType){
addClass.call(this, fadeInClass);
},
NOOP,
function(fadeType){
removeClass.call(this, fadeInClass);
},
NOOP
];
var ONLY_IN = [
NOOP,
function(fadeType){
addClass.call(this, fadeType.cl);
addClass.call(this, fadeInClass);
},
function(fadeType){
removeClass.call(this, fadeType.cl);
removeClass.call(this, fadeInClass);
},
NOOP,
NOOP
];
var ONLY_OUT = [
NOOP,
NOOP,
NOOP,
function(fadeType){
addClass.call(this, fadeType.out);
addClass.call(this, fadeOutClass);
},
function(fadeType){
removeClass.call(this, fadeType.out);
removeClass.call(this, fadeOutClass);
}
];
var Fade = function(fadeType, onShow, onHide){
return function() {
if (!fadeType) { return; }
onShow = onShow !== false;
onHide = onHide !== false;
var oldShow = this.show;
var oldHide = this.hide;
var fns = onShow && onHide ? BOTH : onShow ? ONLY_IN : ONLY_OUT;
fns[0].call(this, fadeType);
onShow && (this.show = function() {
var args = arguments;
oldShow && oldShow.apply(this, args);
fns[1].call(this, fadeType);
setTimeout(function(){
fns[2].call(this, fadeType);
}.bind(this), fadeType.len);
}.bind(this));
onHide && (this.hide = function() {
var args = arguments;
fns[3].call(this, fadeType);
setTimeout(function() {
fns[4].call(this, fadeType);
oldHide && oldHide.apply(this, args);
}.bind(this), fadeType.len);
}.bind(this));
};
};
Fade.NONE = {cl: 'fade_none', out: 'fade_out_none', len: 0};
Fade.SHORT = {cl: 'fade_short', out: 'fade_out_short', len: 250};
Fade.NORMAL = {cl: 'fade_normal', out: 'fade_out_normal', len: 500};
Fade.LONG = {cl: 'fade_long', out: 'fade_out_long', len: 1000};
return Fade;
});
require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {
var define = placements.define.bind(placements,'global_nav_action_trips','handlers',['handlers']);
/**

define([
'placement', 'lib/jquery-amd', 'api-mod', 'page-model', 'common/Radio',
'ta/Core/TA.Record', 'utils/localstorage', 'common/DustRenderer',

], function(

Position, Flyout, DestroyOnHide, AutoReposition, Fade
) {

var oldOverlay = null;
var overlays = {};
var $root = $('#' + placement.id);

var csrf_token = require('page-model').JS_SECURITY_TOKEN;
var servletName = require('page-model').session.pageServlet;
var _getRecentLocations = function(onSuccess) {
$.ajax({
type: 'GET',
url: '/data/1.0/recent/locations',
data: {
limit: 21
},
beforeSend: function(xhr) {

},

});
};

type: 'GET',

limit: 3
},
beforeSend: function(xhr) {
xhr.setRequestHeader('X-Requested-By', csrf_token);

success: onSuccess
});

type: 'GET',
url: '/data/1.0/trips/item',
data: {
limit: 2
},
beforeSend: function(xhr) {
xhr.setRequestHeader('X-Requested-By', csrf_token);
},
success: onSuccess
});
};
var _isTimeWithin2Hours = function(time) {
return (new Date().getTime() - time) < (2 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
};
var _isTimeWithin30Days = function(time) {
return (new Date().getTime() - time) < (30 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
};
var _displayOverlay = function($contentElement) {
var overlayMixins = [
new Flyout($contentElement[0], 'global-nav-flyout global-nav-utility my-trips-dropdown-test-flyout'),

DestroyOnHide,

var _isOverlayOnPage = function() {
// Detect if there is any existing overlay, notification popup or qualaroo survery on the page
return $.find('.ui_notification_container').length || $.find('.ui_overlay').length || $.find('#qual_ol').length;
};
var _showTest1IfNeeded = function(isInControl, storageKey) {
// Current page is POI detail
if (!/Hotel_Review|Attraction_Review|Restaurant_Review/.test(servletName)) {
return;
}
_getRecentLocations(function(response) {
if (response.data && response.data.length > 2 && _isTimeWithin2Hours(response.data[2].date)) {
if (_isOverlayOnPage()) {
Storage.set(STORAGE_SKIP_KEY, true);
return;
}
if (!isInControl) {
_displayOverlay($testEl);
}
Storage.set(storageKey, true);
Tracking.trackEventOnPage(storageKey, "flyout_shown", servletName + "|recents_" + response.data.length, 0, false);
}
});
};
var _showTest2IfNeeded = function(isInControl, storageKey) {
_getRecentLocations(function(response) {
if (response.data && response.data.length >= 2 && !_isTimeWithin2Hours(response.data[1].date)) {
if (_isOverlayOnPage()) {
Storage.set(STORAGE_SKIP_KEY, true);
return;
}
if (!isInControl) {
var message = DustRenderer('saves_masthead_dropdown_test2_string', {numOfItems: response.data.length});
$testEl.find('.test-content').html(message);
_displayOverlay($testEl);
}
Storage.set(storageKey, true);
Tracking.trackEventOnPage(storageKey, "flyout_shown", servletName + "|recents_" + response.data.length, 0, false);
}
});
};
var _showTest3IfNeeded = function(isInControl, storageKey) {
if (servletName === 'Hotel_Review') {
return;
}
_getRecentLocations(function(response) {
if (response.data && response.data.length >= 2 && !_isTimeWithin2Hours(response.data[1].date)) {
var openMyTripsIfNeeded = function(isInControl, storageKey) {
if (_isOverlayOnPage()) {
Storage.set(STORAGE_SKIP_KEY, true);
return;
}
Storage.set(storageKey, true);
if (!isInControl) {
// Tracking for test group is fired in the "My trips" dropdown
radio.trigger('run-my-trips-test-3');
} else {
Tracking.trackEventOnPage(storageKey, "flyout_shown", servletName + "|recents_" + response.data.length, 0, false);
}
};
if (require('page-model').session.user_id) {
_getTripLists(function(response) {
if (!response.data || response.data.length == 0) {
openMyTripsIfNeeded(isInControl, storageKey);
}
});
} else {
openMyTripsIfNeeded(isInControl, storageKey);
}
}
});
};
var _showTestFlyout = function() {
setTimeout(function() {
if (Storage.has(STORAGE_SKIP_KEY)) {
return;
}
if ($root.find('.test-container')) {
var isTAReferrer = $root.find('.test-container').attr('data-is-ta-referrer');
}
if ($testEl.length) {
var testVersion = $testEl.attr('data-test-version');
var storageKey = STORAGE_TEST_KEY_PREFIX + testVersion;
// Attempt to show the test flyout base on test version
if (testVersion == '1' && !Storage.has(storageKey)) {
_showTest1IfNeeded(false, storageKey);
} else if (testVersion == '2' && !isTAReferrer && !Storage.has(storageKey)) {
_showTest2IfNeeded(false, storageKey);
} else if (testVersion == '3' && !isTAReferrer && !Storage.has(storageKey)) {
_showTest3IfNeeded(false, storageKey);
}
} else if ($controlEl.length) {
// The user could have seen overlay if he/she in test group
if (!Storage.has(STORAGE_CONTROL_KEY_PREFIX + '1')) {
_showTest1IfNeeded(true, STORAGE_CONTROL_KEY_PREFIX + '1');
}
if (!Storage.has(STORAGE_CONTROL_KEY_PREFIX + '2') && !isTAReferrer) {
_showTest2IfNeeded(true, STORAGE_CONTROL_KEY_PREFIX + '2');
}
if (!Storage.has(STORAGE_CONTROL_KEY_PREFIX + '3') && !isTAReferrer) {
_showTest3IfNeeded(true, STORAGE_CONTROL_KEY_PREFIX + '3');
}
}
}, 800);
};
var _showQuickSaveFlyout = function() {
setTimeout(function() {
if (!_isOverlayOnPage()
&& $quickSaveEl.length > 0
&& Storage.has(STORAGE_QUICK_SAVE_KEY)
&& !Storage.get(STORAGE_QUICK_SAVE_KEY)
&& api.scrollTop() == 0) {
_displayOverlay($quickSaveEl);
Storage.set(STORAGE_QUICK_SAVE_KEY, true);
Tracking.trackEventOnPage(STORAGE_QUICK_SAVE_KEY, "flyout_shown", servletName, 0, false);
}
}, 1000);
};
radio.on('hide-overlays', function(overlayName){

overlays[overlayName] && overlays[overlayName].hide('hide-overlay') && (overlays[overlayName] = null);
} else {
oldOverlay && oldOverlay.hide('replace-el');
}
});

overlay.domParent = globalNavMenus.find('.global-nav-overlays-container')[0];
overlay.show();
onSuccess && onSuccess(overlay);
oldOverlay = overlay;
overlayName && (overlays[overlayName] = overlay);
});
});
radio.on('run-quick-save-test', function() {
if (Storage.has(STORAGE_QUICK_SAVE_KEY)) {
return;
}
_getTripItems(function(response) {

// Run the test if user hasn't saved in 30 days
Storage.set(STORAGE_QUICK_SAVE_KEY, false);
_showQuickSaveFlyout();
}
});
});
if (Storage.enabled) {
if (document.readyState === 'complete') {
_showQuickSaveFlyout();
} else {
$(window).ready(_showQuickSaveFlyout);
}
}
});

require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {
var define = placements.define.bind(placements,'global_nav_links','handlers',['handlers']);
/* jshint newcap:false */
define([
'placement',
'lib/jquery-amd'
], function(
placement,
$
) {
'use strict';
var placementEl = $('#' + placement.id);
var globalNavMenus = $('[data-placement-name="global_nav_menus"]');
// Tracking: Catch-all
var _trackNavClick = function(elmt, category) {
var trackingLabel = $(elmt).data('trackingLabel');
// Handle links to /# (Help Center) or links opening new window
require(['trjs!ta/Core/TA.Record'], function(taRecord) {
if(/\/#\s*$/.test(elmt.href) || elmt.target == '_blank') {
taRecord.trackEventOnPage(category, 'click', trackingLabel);
} else {
taRecord.setEvtCookie(category, 'click', trackingLabel, 0, elmt.href);
}
});
};
// Tracking: Catches all of the non-submenu links that require tracking
// Links only qualify if they have the data-tracking-label attribute.
globalNavMenus.on('click', 'a.global-nav-link[data-tracking-label]', function() {
_trackNavClick(this, 'TopNav');
});
// Tracking for links in submenus works by looking up the active-menu-trigger
// (link that triggered the dropdown) and using it's tracking-label as a prefix
globalNavMenus.on('click', 'a.subLink', function() {
var triggerEl = $("[data-active-menu-trigger][data-tracking-label]", placementEl);
var trackingLabel = triggerEl.data('trackingLabel') + "_sublink";
_trackNavClick(this, 'TopNav');
});
});

require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {
var define = placements.define.bind(placements,'saves_cta_highlights','handlers',['handlers']);
/**
* Created by huihongwang on 7/5/17.
*/
define([
'placement', 'lib/jquery-amd', 'page-model',
'ta/Core/TA.Record', 'utils/localstorage',
'overlays/Overlay',
'overlays/position', 'overlays/styles/flyout', 'overlays/options/fade', 'overlays/options/autoReposition'
], function(
placement, $, pageModel,
Tracking, Storage,
Overlay,
Position, Flyout, Fade, AutoReposition
) {
'use strict';
var overlay;
var $root = $('#' + placement.id);
var $testEl = $root.find('.saves-cta-highlights-test');
var $controlEl = $root.find('.saves-cta-highlights-control');
var STORAGE_TEST_KEY_PREFIX = 'saves-cta-highlights-test';
var STORAGE_CONTROL_KEY_PREFIX = 'saves-cta-highlights-control';
var STORAGE_SKIP_KEY = 'saves-cta-highlights-skip';
var csrf_token = require('page-model').JS_SECURITY_TOKEN;
var servletName = require('page-model').session.pageServlet;
var _isTimeWithinXHours = function(hours, time) {
return (new Date().getTime() - time) < (hours * 60 * 60 * 1000);
};
var _displayOverlay = function() {
$testEl.on('click', '.ui_close_x', function() {
overlay && overlay.destroy() && (overlay = null);
});
$root.parent().on('click', '.saves-widget-button', function() {
overlay && overlay.destroy() && (overlay = null);
});
overlay = new Overlay($root.parent()[0], [
new Flyout($testEl[0], 'saves-cta-highlights-test-flyout ui_popover'),
Position.bottomLeft([-10, 15]),
AutoReposition,
Fade(Fade.SHORT, true, true)
]);
overlay.show();
};
var _getRecentLocations = function(onSuccess) {
$.ajax({
type: 'GET',
url: '/data/1.0/recent/locations',
data: {
limit: 3
},
beforeSend: function(xhr) {
xhr.setRequestHeader('X-Requested-By', csrf_token);
},
success: onSuccess
});
};
var _getTripItems = function(onSuccess) {
$.ajax({
type: 'GET',
url: '/data/1.0/trips/item',
data: {
limit: 1
},
beforeSend: function(xhr) {
xhr.setRequestHeader('X-Requested-By', csrf_token);
},
success: onSuccess
});
};
var _runTestIfNeeded = function(isControlGroup, storageKey) {
var trackingLabel = '';
if (!require('page-model').session.loggedIn) {
// Run the test if user is logged out
trackingLabel = 'logged_out|' + servletName;
if (!isControlGroup) {
_displayOverlay();
}
Storage.set(storageKey, true);
Tracking.trackEventOnPage(storageKey, "flyout_shown", trackingLabel, 0, false);
return;
}
_getRecentLocations(function(response) {
if (response.data && response.data.length > 1 && _isTimeWithinXHours(2, response.data[1].date)
&& (response.data.length <= 2 || !_isTimeWithinXHours(2, response.data[2].date))) {
// This is the 2nd page user visited in last 2 hours
_getTripItems(function(response) {
if (!response.data || response.data.length == 0) {
trackingLabel = 'never_saved|' + servletName;
} else if (!_isTimeWithinXHours(30 * 24, new Date(response.data[0].created).getTime())) {
trackingLabel = 'no_save_last_30_days|' + servletName;
} else {
Storage.set(STORAGE_SKIP_KEY, true);
return;
}
// Run the test if user is visiting the 2nd location detail page in last 2 hours
// and haven't saved in last 30 days
if (!isControlGroup) {
_displayOverlay();
}
Storage.set(storageKey, true);
Tracking.trackEventOnPage(storageKey, "flyout_shown", trackingLabel, 0, false);
});
}
});
};
// Detect if there is any existing overlay, notification popup or qualaroo survery on the page
var _isOverlayOnPage = function() {
return $.find('.ui_notification_container').length || $.find('.ui_overlay').length || $.find('#qual_ol').length;
};
var _showTestFlyout = function() {
setTimeout(function() {
if (Storage.has(STORAGE_SKIP_KEY)) {
return;
}
if (_isOverlayOnPage()) {
Storage.set(STORAGE_SKIP_KEY, true);
return;
}
if (pageModel.session.pageServlet === 'Hotel_Review' && require.defined('hotels/hrSurveys') && require('hotels/hrSurveys').shouldShowSurvey()) {
return;
}
if ($testEl.length) {
var testVersion = $testEl.attr('data-test-version');
var storageKey = STORAGE_TEST_KEY_PREFIX + testVersion;
if (!Storage.has(storageKey)) {
_runTestIfNeeded(false, storageKey);
}
} else if ($controlEl.length) {
// The user could have seen overlay if he/she in test group
var storageKey = STORAGE_CONTROL_KEY_PREFIX;
if (!Storage.has(storageKey)) {
_runTestIfNeeded(true, storageKey);
}
}
}, 1600);
};
if (Storage.enabled) {
if (document.readyState === 'complete') {
_showTestFlyout();
} else {
$(window).ready(_showTestFlyout);
}
}
});

require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {
var define = placements.define.bind(placements,'hsx_special_messaging','handlers',['handlers']);
/*
* Private javascript for hsx_special_messaging placement
*/
define(["placement", "ta/Core/TA.Event", 'ta/prwidgets'],
function(placement, taEvent, prwidgets) {
var eventName = 'update-' + placement.name;
/**
* Called on data-targetEvent update-<placementname>
*
* @param {DocumentFragment} contentDiv - A DOM element containing the new special messaging placement
*/
function _updatePlacement(contentDiv) {
// Normalize contentDiv - sometimes desired content is root, sometimes a child (ex. FiltersUtil.js vs Repoll.js)
if (contentDiv && contentDiv.getAttribute('data-targetEvent') != eventName) {
contentDiv = contentDiv.querySelector('[data-targetEvent="' + eventName + '"]');
}
var placementDiv = document.getElementById(placement.id);
if(!contentDiv || !placementDiv) {
return;
}
placementDiv.innerHTML = contentDiv.outerHTML;
prwidgets.initWidgets(placementDiv);
}
taEvent.on(eventName, _updatePlacement);
return {
};
});

require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {
var define = placements.define.bind(placements,'browser_mode_tracking','handlers',['handlers']);
define([
'placement', 'ta/Core/TA.Event', 'ta/Browser', 'ta/Core/TA.Record', 'ta/util/SessionStorage'
], function(placement, taEvent, taBrowser, taRecord, taSessionStorage){
var browserName;
var sessionStoreKey = placement.id + '_browser_mode_tracked';
function _trackBrowserMode (resultStr) {
taRecord.trackEventOnPage('BROWSER_TRACKING', browserName, resultStr, null, true);
}
taEvent.queueForLoad(function(){
if (taSessionStorage.canUseSessionStore() && sessionStorage.getItem(sessionStoreKey)) {
// already tracked
return;
}
else {
if (taBrowser.isChrome()) {
browserName = "Chrome";
taBrowser.isChromeIncognito(_trackBrowserMode);
taSessionStorage.canUseSessionStore() && sessionStorage.setItem(sessionStoreKey, '1');
}
}
});

require(['ta/p13n/placements'], function(placements) {
var define = placements.define.bind(placements,'document_cookie_banner','handlers',['handlers']);
define([
'placement', 'lib/jquery-amd', 'ta/util/Cookie', 'ta/Core/TA.Event',
'ta/popups/PopUtil'
], function(
placement, $, taCookie, taEvent,
PopUtil
){
'use strict';
taEvent.queueForAfterLoad(function(){
var $placement = $('#' + placement.id);
$(document.body).prepend($placement);
$placement.find('p span')
.on('click', function(){
PopUtil.cookieSettingsPanel();
});
$placement.addClass('showing');
var smartbanner = $('#smartbanner');
if (smartbanner[0]) {
$placement.addClass('smart-banner-top');
}
$placement.css({
marginTop: -$placement.height()
}).animate({marginTop: 0}, {
duration: 'long',
complete: function() {
taEvent.fireEvent("showingCookieConsentBanner");
}
});
// Drop a cookie to signify that the banner has been shown to the user.
// This cookie is checked on the server.
taCookie.write('cookieconsent', '1', taCookie.ONE_HOUR);
}, 'placement: document_cookie_consent');
});
